Precise translation of phrases or learning new words has secondary importance. Searching for words in a dictionary must be avoided because it means loss of time and concentration. In the real-life situations, there is no time for looking into dictionary anyway, so get used to it. During the second round of translation, you will probably be able to translate more phrases.
